/**
 * Generate next available UID for new user
 * Format: U-{6-digit sequential number}
 *
 * IMPORTANT: Orders by UID (not createdAt) to prevent race conditions
 * where users created at similar times could get duplicate UIDs
 */
export async function generateNextUID(): Promise<string> {
  const supabase = createClient();

  // Get the user with the highest UID number (ordered DESC by uid field)
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('users')
    .select('uid')
    .order('uid', { ascending: false })
    .limit(1)
    .maybeSingle(); // Use maybeSingle() instead of single() to handle 0 rows gracefully

  let nextNumber = 1;

  if (!error && data?.uid) {
    // Extract number from UID (e.g., "U-000123" -> 123)
    // Only match exactly 6-digit UIDs to avoid timestamp-based UIDs
    const match = data.uid.match(/^U-(\d{6})$/);
    if (match) {
      nextNumber = parseInt(match[1], 10) + 1;
    }
  }

  // Format as U-{6-digit number}
  return `U-${nextNumber.toString().padStart(6, '0')}`;
}

/**
 * Create a new user
 * Supports both email and phone registration
 */
export async function createUser(data: {
  email?: string;
  phone?: string;
  password?: string;
  name: string;
}): Promise<UserWithoutPassword> {
  const { email, password, name } = data;
  const rawPhone = data.phone;
  const phone = rawPhone ? normalizePhoneNumber(rawPhone) : rawPhone;

  log.info('Creating user', { email, phone, name });

  try {
    // Validate at least one identifier
    if (!email && !phone) {
      throw new Error('Email or phone number is required.');
    }

    // Validate email if provided
    if (email && !validateEmail(email)) {
      log.warn('Invalid email format', { email });
      throw new Error('Invalid email format.');
    }

    // Validate phone if provided
    if (phone && !validatePhone(phone)) {
      log.warn('Invalid phone format', { phone });
      throw new Error('Invalid phone number format.');
    }

    // Validate password (required for email, optional for phone)
    if (password && !validatePassword(password)) {
      log.warn('Invalid password length', { email, phone });
      throw new Error('Password must be at least 8 characters.');
    }

    // Check if user already exists
    const exists = await checkUserExists({ email, phone });
    if (exists) {
      log.warn('User already exists', { email, phone });
      throw new Error(
        'An account with this email or phone number already exists.'
      );
    }

    // Hash password if provided
    const hashedPassword = password ? await hashPassword(password) : null;

    const supabase = createClient();

    // Create user with retry logic for UID conflicts (race condition handling)
    let user;
    let retries = 0;
    const maxRetries = 3;

    while (retries < maxRetries) {
      try {
        // Generate next UID
        const uid = await generateNextUID();

        // Attempt to create user
        const now = new Date().toISOString();
        const { data: createdUser, error: createError } = await supabase
          .from('users')
          .insert({
            id: randomUUID(),
            uid,
            email: email || null,
            phone: phone || null,
            password: hashedPassword,
            name,
            role: 'USER',
            isVerified: true, // All users are verified via OTP (email or phone)
            updatedAt: now,
          })
          .select()
          .single();

        if (createError) {
          // Check if error is due to unique constraint violation on UID
          if (
            createError.code === '23505' &&
            createError.message?.includes('uid')
          ) {
            // UID conflict - retry with new UID
            retries++;
            log.warn('UID conflict detected, retrying', {
              retries,
              email,
              phone,
            });

            if (retries >= maxRetries) {
              log.error('Max retries reached for UID generation', {
                email,
                phone,
              });
              throw new Error('Unable to create user ID.');
            }

            // Wait a bit before retrying to reduce collision probability
            await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100 * retries));
            continue;
          }

          // Other error - throw
          throw createError;
        }

        user = createdUser;
        // Success - break out of retry loop
        break;
      } catch (error) {
        // If it's not a UID conflict error, rethrow
        if (
          retries >= maxRetries ||
          !(error instanceof Error && error.message?.includes('uid'))
        ) {
          throw error;
        }
      }
    }

    if (!user) {
      throw new Error('Unable to create user.');
    }

    log.info('User created successfully', {
      userId: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      phone: user.phone,
      role: user.role,
    });

    // Link any orphaned guest transactions with this phone number
    if (phone) {
      try {
        const linkedCount = await linkOrphanedTransactions(
          user.id,
          rawPhone ?? phone
        );
        if (linkedCount > 0) {
          log.info('Linked orphaned transactions to new user', {
            userId: user.id,
            phone,
            count: linkedCount,
          });
        }
      } catch (error) {
        log.error('Failed to link orphaned transactions during user creation', {
          userId: user.id,
          phone,
import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
import { getPhoneLookupCandidates } from '@/lib/utils/text';

/**
 * User information type (without password)
 */
export type UserInfo = {
  id: string;
  uid: string;
  email: string | null;
  phone: string | null;
  name: string;
  role: 'USER' | 'ADMIN';
  isVerified: boolean;
  shippingAddress: string | null;
  postalCode: string | null;
  createdAt: Date;
  updatedAt: Date;
};

/**
 * Generic user query function
 * Reduces duplication in getUserById, getUserByEmail, getUserByPhone
 */
export async function queryUser(where: {
  id?: string;
  email?: string;
  phone?: string;
}): Promise<UserInfo | null> {
  const supabase = createClient();

  let query = supabase
    .from('users')
    .select(
      'id, uid, email, phone, name, role, isVerified, shippingAddress, postalCode, createdAt, updatedAt'
    )
    .limit(1);

  if (where.id) {
    query = query.eq('id', where.id);
  } else if (where.email) {
    query = query.eq('email', where.email);
  } else if (where.phone) {
    query = query.eq('phone', where.phone);
  } else {
    return null;
  }

  const { data, error } = await query.single();

  if (error || !data) {
    return null;
  }

  // Convert string dates to Date objects for type compatibility
  return {
    ...data,
    createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
    updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
  };
}

/**
 * Check if a user exists with the given identifier
 * Used for uniqueness validation
 */
export async function checkUserExists(
  identifier: { email?: string; phone?: string },
  excludeUserId?: string
): Promise<boolean> {
  const supabase = createClient();

  // Build OR conditions
  const conditions = [];

  if (identifier.email) {
    conditions.push(`email.eq.${identifier.email}`);
  }

  if (identifier.phone) {
    for (const phone of getPhoneLookupCandidates(identifier.phone)) {
      conditions.push(`phone.eq.${phone}`);
    }
  }

  if (conditions.length === 0) {
    return false;
  }

  let query = supabase
    .from('users')
    .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
    .or(conditions.join(','));

  if (excludeUserId) {
    query = query.neq('id', excludeUserId);
  }

  const { count, error } = await query;

  if (error) {
    return false;
  }

  return (count ?? 0) > 0;
}

/**
 * Get user by ID
 */
export async function getUserById(userId: string): Promise<UserInfo | null> {
  return queryUser({ id: userId });
}

/**
 * Get user by email
 */
export async function getUserByEmail(email: string): Promise<UserInfo | null> {
  return queryUser({ email });
}

/**
 * Get user by phone
 */
export async function getUserByPhone(phone: string): Promise<UserInfo | null> {
  for (const lookupPhone of getPhoneLookupCandidates(phone)) {
    const user = await queryUser({ phone: lookupPhone });
    if (user) return user;
  }

  return null;
}

/**
 * Get user by identifier (email or phone)
 */
export async function getUserByIdentifier(
  identifier: string
): Promise<UserInfo | null> {
  const type = detectIdentifierType(identifier);

  if (type === 'email') {
    return getUserByEmail(identifier);
  } else if (type === 'phone') {
    return getUserByPhone(identifier);
  }

  return null;
}

/**
 * Update user's shipping information
 */
export async function updateUserShippingInfo(
  userId: string,
  data: {
    shippingAddress: string;
    postalCode?: string;
  }
): Promise<void> {
  log.info('Updating user shipping info', { userId });

  try {
    const supabase = createClient();

    const { error } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .update({
        shippingAddress: data.shippingAddress,
        postalCode: data.postalCode,
      })
      .eq('id', userId);

    if (error) {
      log.error('Failed to update user shipping info', { userId, error });
      // Don't throw error - this is a non-critical update
      return;
    }

    log.info('User shipping info updated successfully', { userId });
  } catch (error) {
    log.error('Failed to update user shipping info', {
      userId,
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
    });
    // Don't throw error - this is a non-critical update
  }
}

/**
 * Update user profile information
 */
export async function updateUserProfile(
  userId: string,
  data: {
    name?: string;
    email?: string;
    phone?: string;
    shippingAddress?: string;
    postalCode?: string;
  }
): Promise<UserInfo> {
  log.info('Updating user profile', { userId, fields: Object.keys(data) });

  try {
    // Validate email uniqueness
    await validateEmailUniqueness(data.email, userId);

    const phone = data.phone ? normalizePhoneNumber(data.phone) : data.phone;

    // Validate phone uniqueness
    await validatePhoneUniqueness(phone, userId);

    const supabase = createClient();

    // Build update object
    const updateData: Record<string, unknown> = {};
    if (data.name !== undefined) updateData.name = data.name;
    if (data.email !== undefined) updateData.email = data.email || null;
    if (data.phone !== undefined) updateData.phone = phone || null;
    if (data.shippingAddress !== undefined)
      updateData.shippingAddress = data.shippingAddress;
    if (data.postalCode !== undefined) updateData.postalCode = data.postalCode;

    // Update user
    const { data: updatedUser, error } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .update(updateData)
      .eq('id', userId)
      .select(
        'id, uid, email, phone, name, role, isVerified, shippingAddress, postalCode, createdAt, updatedAt'
      )
      .single();

    if (error || !updatedUser) {
      log.error('Failed to update user profile', { userId, error });
      throw new Error('Unable to update profile.');
    }

    log.info('User profile updated successfully', { userId });

    // Convert dates
    return {
      ...updatedUser,
      createdAt: new Date(updatedUser.createdAt),
      updatedAt: new Date(updatedUser.updatedAt),
    };
  } catch (error) {
    log.error('Failed to update user profile', {
      userId,
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
    });
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Change user password
 * SECURITY: Always requires current password verification if user has a password
 */
export async function changeUserPassword(
  userId: string,
  currentPassword: string,
  newPassword: string
): Promise<void> {
  log.info('Changing user password', { userId });

  try {
    // Verify current password (security check)
    await verifyCurrentPassword(userId, currentPassword);

    // Update password
    await updatePassword(userId, newPassword);

    log.info('User password changed successfully', { userId });
  } catch (error) {
    log.error('Failed to change user password', {
      userId,
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
    });
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Reset password via OTP verification (for users who don't know their current password)
 * This is for users who registered via OTP checkout with auto-generated passwords
 */
export async function resetPasswordWithOTP(
  userId: string,
  newPassword: string
): Promise<void> {
  log.info('Resetting password via OTP', { userId });

  try {
    // Verify user exists
    const user = await getUserWithPassword(userId);
    if (!user) {
      log.warn('User not found', { userId });
      throw new Error('User not found.');
    }

    // Update password (validation happens inside)
    await updatePassword(userId, newPassword);

    log.info('Password reset successfully via OTP', { userId });
  } catch (error) {
    log.error('Failed to reset password', {
      userId,
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
    });
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Set password for OTP-only users
 */
export async function setUserPassword(
  userId: string,
  newPassword: string
): Promise<void> {
  log.info('Setting user password', { userId });

  try {
    // Ensure user doesn't already have a password
    await ensureNoPassword(userId);

    // Update password (validation happens inside)
    await updatePassword(userId, newPassword);

    log.info('User password set successfully', { userId });
  } catch (error) {
    log.error('Failed to set user password', {
      userId,
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
    });
    throw error;
  }
}

/**
 * Link orphaned guest transactions to a user account
 * This is called when a user registers/logs in with OTP to ensure
 * any previous guest transactions with their phone are linked to their account
 */
export async function linkOrphanedTransactions(
  userId: string,
  phone: string
): Promise<number> {
  const normalizedPhone = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
  const phoneLookupCandidates = getPhoneLookupCandidates(phone);

  log.info('Linking orphaned guest transactions to user', {
    userId,
    phone: normalizedPhone,
  });

  try {
    const supabase = createClient();

    // Find all guest transactions with this phone that don't have a userId
    const { data: orphanedTransactions, error: fetchError } = await supabase
      .from('transactions')
      .select('id, transactionCode')
      .in('phone', phoneLookupCandidates)
      .is('userId', null)
      .eq('isGuest', true);

    if (fetchError) {
      log.error('Failed to fetch orphaned transactions', {
        userId,
        phone: normalizedPhone,
        error: fetchError,
      });
      return 0;
    }

    if (!orphanedTransactions || orphanedTransactions.length === 0) {
      log.info('No orphaned transactions found for user', {
        userId,
        phone: normalizedPhone,
      });
      return 0;
    }

    // Update all orphaned transactions to link them to the user
    // Keep isGuest=true to indicate these were originally guest transactions
    const { error: updateError } = await supabase
      .from('transactions')
      .update({ userId })
      .in('phone', phoneLookupCandidates)
      .is('userId', null)
      .eq('isGuest', true);

    if (updateError) {
      log.error('Failed to update orphaned transactions', {
        userId,
        phone: normalizedPhone,
        error: updateError,
      });
      return 0;
    }

    log.info('Orphaned transactions linked successfully', {
      userId,
      phone: normalizedPhone,
      count: orphanedTransactions.length,
      transactionCodes: orphanedTransactions.map((t) => t.transactionCode),
    });

    return orphanedTransactions.length;
  } catch (error) {
    log.error('Failed to link orphaned transactions', {
      userId,
      phone: normalizedPhone,
      error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
    });
    // Don't throw - this is a best-effort operation
    return 0;
  }
}

/**
 * Get user's transaction history with details
 * Also includes guest transactions that match the user's phone or email
 */
export async function getUserTransactions(
  userId: string,
  options?: {
    limit?: number;
    offset?: number;
    status?: 'PENDING' | 'COMPLETED' | 'FAILED';
  }
) {
  log.info('Fetching user transactions', { userId, options });

  try {
    const { limit = 10, offset = 0, status } = options || {};

    const supabase = createClient();

    // First, get the user's phone and email to also fetch matching guest transactions
    const { data: user, error: userError } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .select('phone, email')
      .eq('id', userId)
      .single();
import 'server-only';
import bcrypt from 'bcryptjs';
import { randomUUID } from 'crypto';
import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
import { log } from '@/lib/logger';
import {
  getPhoneLookupCandidates,
  normalizePhoneNumber,
} from '@/lib/utils/text';

  detectIdentifierType,

  linkOrphanedTransactions,

export interface AuthUser {
  id: string;
  email: string | null;
  phone: string | null;
  name: string;
  role: 'USER' | 'ADMIN';
}

/**
 * Authenticate user with identifier (email or phone) and password
 * @param identifier User email or phone number
 * @param password User password
 * @returns Authenticated user data
 * @throws Error if authentication fails
 */
export async function authenticateUser(
  identifier: string,
  password: string
): Promise<AuthUser> {
  if (!identifier || !password) {
    throw new Error('Email/phone number and password are required.');
  }

  try {
    const identifierType = detectIdentifierType(identifier);

    if (identifierType === 'invalid') {
      throw new Error('Enter a valid email address or phone number.');
    }

    const supabase = createClient();

    // Find user by email or phone
    const userQuery = supabase.from('users').select('*').limit(1);
    const { data: user, error } =
      identifierType === 'email'
        ? await userQuery.eq('email', identifier).maybeSingle()
        : await userQuery
            .in('phone', getPhoneLookupCandidates(identifier))
            .maybeSingle();

    if (error || !user) {
      log.warn('Login attempt with non-existent identifier', {
        identifier,
        identifierType,
      });
      throw new Error('No account was found for those credentials.');
    }

    // Check if user has a password (phone-only users might not have password)
    if (!user.password) {
      log.warn('Login attempt for user without password', {
        identifier,
        userId: user.id,
      });
      throw new Error(
        'This account does not have a password. Use one-time sign-in or set a password first.'
      );
    }

    const isPasswordValid = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);

    if (!isPasswordValid) {
      log.warn('Login attempt with invalid password', {
        identifier,
        userId: user.id,
      });
      throw new Error('Password is incorrect.');
    }

    log.info('User authenticated successfully', {
      identifier,
      userId: user.id,
    });

    return {
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      phone: user.phone,
      name: user.name,
      role: user.role,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof Error) {
      throw error;
    }
    log.error('Authentication error', { identifier, error });
    throw new Error('Unable to authenticate.');
  }
}

/**
 * Authenticate user by phone (OTP-verified, no password)
 * This is called after OTP verification
 * @param phone User phone number
 * @returns Authenticated user data
 * @throws Error if authentication fails
 */
export async function authenticateUserByPhone(
  phone: string
): Promise<AuthUser> {
  if (!phone) {
    throw new Error('Phone number is required.');
  }

  try {
    const normalizedPhone = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
    const phoneLookupCandidates = getPhoneLookupCandidates(phone);
    const supabase = createClient();

    const { data: user, error } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .select('*')
      .in('phone', phoneLookupCandidates)
      .limit(1)
      .maybeSingle();

    if (error || !user) {
      log.warn('Login attempt with non-existent phone', {
        phone: normalizedPhone,
      });
      throw new Error('No account was found for that phone number.');
    }

    log.info('User authenticated successfully via phone', {
      phone: normalizedPhone,
      userId: user.id,
    });

    // Link any orphaned guest transactions with this phone
    try {
      const linkedCount = await linkOrphanedTransactions(user.id, phone);
      if (linkedCount > 0) {
        log.info('Linked orphaned transactions during phone login', {
          userId: user.id,
          phone: normalizedPhone,
          count: linkedCount,
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      log.error('Failed to link orphaned transactions during phone login', {
        userId: user.id,
        phone: normalizedPhone,
        error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
      });
      // Don't fail authentication if linking fails
    }

    return {
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      phone: user.phone,
      name: user.name,
      role: user.role,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof Error) {
      throw error;
    }
    log.error('Phone authentication error', { phone, error });
    throw new Error('Unable to authenticate by phone.');
  }
}

/**
 * Authenticate user by email (OTP-verified, no password)
 * This is called after OTP verification for email-based OTP login
 * @param email User email address
 * @returns Authenticated user data
 * @throws Error if authentication fails
 */
export async function authenticateUserByEmail(
  email: string
): Promise<AuthUser> {
  if (!email) {
    throw new Error('Email is required.');
  }

  try {
    const supabase = createClient();

    const { data: user, error } = await supabase
      .from('users')
      .select('*')
      .eq('email', email)
      .single();

    if (error || !user) {
      log.warn('Login attempt with non-existent email', { email });
      throw new Error('No account was found for that email address.');
    }

    log.info('User authenticated successfully via email', {
      email,
      userId: user.id,
    });

    return {
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      phone: user.phone,
      name: user.name,
      role: user.role,
    };
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof Error) {
      throw error;
    }
    log.error('Email authentication error', { email, error });
    throw new Error('Unable to authenticate by email.');
  }
}

 /**
  * Construct absolute URL from path
  * @param path - Relative or absolute path
  * @returns Absolute URL
  */
 export function getAbsoluteUrl(path: string): string {
   const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
 
   // If path is already absolute, return it
   if (path.startsWith('http://') || path.startsWith('https://')) {
     return path;
   }
 
   // Remove leading slash if present to avoid double slashes
   const cleanPath = path.startsWith('/') ? path : `/${path}`;
 
   return `${baseUrl}${cleanPath}`;
 }

 /**
  * Generate Product JSON-LD structured data
  * Creates rich snippet for product pages with offers, images, and ratings
  */
 export function generateProductSchema(
   product: SchemaProduct,
   selectedVariant?: SchemaVariant
 ): object {
   const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
 
   // Get images from product media or variant media
   const images: string[] = [];
 
   if (selectedVariant?.media && selectedVariant.media.length > 0) {
     // Use selected variant's media
     const variantImages = selectedVariant.media
       .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
       .map((m) => m.url);
     images.push(...variantImages);
   } else if (product.media && product.media.length > 0) {
     // Use product-level media
     const productImages = product.media
       .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
       .map((m) => m.url);
     images.push(...productImages);
   } else if (product.images && product.images.length > 0) {
     // Use legacy images field
     images.push(...product.images);
   } else if (product.variants && product.variants.length > 0) {
     // Fallback: collect images from all variants if product has no direct media
     for (const variant of product.variants) {
       if (variant.media && variant.media.length > 0) {
         const variantImages = variant.media
           .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
           .map((m) => m.url);
         images.push(...variantImages);
       }
     }
   }
 
   // Calculate final price (with variant adjustment if applicable)
   let finalPrice = product.price;
   if (selectedVariant) {
     finalPrice += selectedVariant.priceAdjust;
   }
 
   // Apply discount if exists
   if (product.discount && product.discount > 0) {
     finalPrice = finalPrice * (1 - product.discount / 100);
   }
 
   // Determine stock availability
   let stock = product.stock;
   if (selectedVariant) {
     stock = selectedVariant.stock;
   }
 
   const availability =
     stock > 0 ? 'https://schema.org/InStock' : 'https://schema.org/OutOfStock';
 
   // Schema.org requires at least one image - use logo as absolute last resort
-  const schemaImages = images.length > 0 ? images : [`${baseUrl}/logo.png`];
+  const schemaImages =
+    images.length > 0
+      ? images.map((image) => toAbsoluteUrl(image, baseUrl))
+      : [`${baseUrl}/images/og-default.svg`];
 
   const schema = {
     '@context': 'https://schema.org',
     '@type': 'Product',
     name: selectedVariant
       ? `${product.name} - ${selectedVariant.name}`
       : product.name,
-    description:
-      product.description || `${product.name} - خرید آنلاین از کیتیا`,
+    description: product.description || `${product.name} - ${siteConfig.name}`,
     image: schemaImages,
     ...(product.sku && { sku: product.sku }),
     brand: {
       '@type': 'Brand',
-      name: 'کیتیا',
+      name: siteConfig.name,
     },
     offers: {
       '@type': 'Offer',
       price: finalPrice.toString(),
-      priceCurrency: 'IRR',
+      priceCurrency: siteLocale.currency,
       availability,
       url: `${baseUrl}/products/${product.slug || product.id}`,
       ...(product.discount &&
         product.discount > 0 && {
           priceValidUntil: new Date(
             Date.now() + 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000
           ).toISOString(), // 30 days
         }),
     },
   };
 
   return schema;
 }

     5	import { siteConfig, siteLocale } from '@/config/site';
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Get the base URL for the application
     9	 * Uses environment variables with fallback to production URL
    10	 */
    11	export function getBaseUrl(): string {
    12	  // Check if we're on the server side
    13	  if (typeof window === 'undefined') {
    14	    // Server-side: use environment variable or production URL
    15	
    16	    // Priority 1: Use NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL if set (allows dynamic configuration in Vercel)
    17	    const siteUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL;
    18	    if (siteUrl) {
    19	      return siteUrl;
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    // Priority 2: Use NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL when configured.
    23	    const appUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL;
    24	    if (
    25	      appUrl &&
    26	      (process.env.VERCEL_ENV !== 'production' || !appUrl.includes('localhost'))
    27	    ) {
    28	      return appUrl;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    // Priority 3: Use VERCEL_URL for preview or production deployments.
    32	    const vercelUrl = process.env.VERCEL_URL;
    33	    if (vercelUrl && !vercelUrl.includes('localhost')) {
    34	      return `https://${vercelUrl}`;
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    // Fallback for local development.
    38	    return 'http://localhost:3000';
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  // Client-side: use window.location.origin
    42	  return window.location.origin;
    43	}
    44	
    45	/**
    46	 * Construct absolute URL from path
    47	 * @param path - Relative or absolute path
    48	 * @returns Absolute URL
    49	 */
    50	export function getAbsoluteUrl(path: string): string {
    51	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
    52	
    53	  // If path is already absolute, return it
    54	  if (path.startsWith('http://') || path.startsWith('https://')) {
    55	    return path;
    56	  }
    57	
    58	  // Remove leading slash if present to avoid double slashes
    59	  const cleanPath = path.startsWith('/') ? path : `/${path}`;
    60	
    61	  return `${baseUrl}${cleanPath}`;
    62	}
    63

    70	  defaultTitle: siteConfig.name,
    71	  defaultDescription: siteConfig.description,
    72	} as const;

    56	function escapeHtml(value: unknown): string {
    57	  return String(value ?? '')
    58	    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
    59	    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    60	    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
    61	    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
    62	    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
    63	}

   108	async function sendEmail(options: {
   109	  to: string;
   110	  subject: string;
   111	  html: string;
   112	  text: string;
   113	}): Promise<SendEmailResult> {
   114	  const from =
   115	    process.env.EMAIL_FROM ||
   116	    `${siteName} <${process.env.EMAIL_FROM_ADDRESS || 'noreply@example.com'}>`;
   117	
   118	  const useResendSmtp =
   119	    process.env.RESEND_SMTP === 'true' ||
   120	    !!process.env.RESEND_SMTP_HOST ||
   121	    !!process.env.RESEND_SMTP_USER ||
   122	    !!process.env.RESEND_SMTP_PASS;
   123	
   124	  try {
   125	    let transporter: nodemailer.Transporter;
   126	
   127	    if (useResendSmtp) {
   128	      const smtpPass =
   129	        process.env.RESEND_SMTP_PASS || process.env.RESEND_API_KEY;
   130	
   131	      if (!smtpPass) {
   132	        throw new Error('RESEND_SMTP_PASS or RESEND_API_KEY is required');
   133	      }
   134	
   135	      transporter = nodemailer.createTransport({
   136	        host: process.env.RESEND_SMTP_HOST || 'smtp.resend.com',
   137	        port: parseInt(process.env.RESEND_SMTP_PORT || '587'),
   138	        secure: process.env.RESEND_SMTP_SECURE === 'true',
   139	        auth: {
   140	          user: process.env.RESEND_SMTP_USER || 'resend',
   141	          pass: smtpPass,
   142	        },
   143	      });
   144	    } else if (process.env.EMAIL_SMTP_HOST) {
   145	      transporter = nodemailer.createTransport({
   146	        host: process.env.EMAIL_SMTP_HOST,
   147	        port: parseInt(process.env.EMAIL_SMTP_PORT || '587'),
   148	        secure: process.env.EMAIL_SMTP_SECURE === 'true',
   149	        auth: {
   150	          user: process.env.EMAIL_SMTP_USER,
   151	          pass: process.env.EMAIL_SMTP_PASS,
   152	        },
   153	      });
   154	    } else if (resend) {
   155	      const { data, error } = await resend.emails.send({
   156	        from,
   157	        to: options.to,
   158	        subject: options.subject,
   159	        html: options.html,
   160	        text: options.text,
   161	      });
   162	
   163	      if (error) {
   164	        log.error('Resend API error', { error: error.message });
   165	        return { success: false, error: error.message };
   166	      }
   167	
   168	      log.info('Email sent via Resend API', {
   169	        to: options.to,
   170	        messageId: data?.id,
   171	      });
   172	
   173	      return { success: true, messageId: data?.id };
   174	    } else {
   175	      const testAccount = await nodemailer.createTestAccount();
   176	      log.info('Created Ethereal test account', { user: testAccount.user });
   177	
   178	      transporter = nodemailer.createTransport({
   179	        host: 'smtp.ethereal.email',
   180	        port: 587,
   181	        secure: false,
   182	        auth: {
   183	          user: testAccount.user,
   184	          pass: testAccount.pass,
   185	        },
   186	      });
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    const info = await transporter.sendMail({
   190	      from,
   191	      to: options.to,
   192	      subject: options.subject,
   193	      text: options.text,
   194	      html: options.html,
   195	    });
   196	
   197	    if (
   198	      !process.env.EMAIL_SMTP_HOST &&
   199	      !useResendSmtp &&
   200	      !resend &&
   201	      info.messageId
   202	    ) {
   203	      const previewUrl = nodemailer.getTestMessageUrl(info);
   204	      if (previewUrl) {
   205	        log.info('Email sent to Ethereal test inbox', {
   206	          to: options.to,
   207	          subject: options.subject,
   208	          previewUrl,
   209	          messageId: info.messageId,
   210	        });
   211	      }
   212	    }
   213	
   214	    return { success: true, messageId: info.messageId };
   215	  } catch (err) {
   216	    const errorMessage = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error';
   217	    log.error('Failed to send email', { error: errorMessage });
   218	    return { success: false, error: errorMessage };
   219	  }
   220	}

   222	export async function sendOTPEmail(
   223	  email: string,
   224	  otp: string
   225	): Promise<SendEmailResult> {
   226	  const safeOtp = escapeHtml(otp);
   227	  const title = `Your ${siteName} sign-in code`;
   228	  const html = layoutEmail(
   229	    title,
   230	    `
   231	      <p>Use this verification code to finish signing in to ${escapeHtml(siteName)}.</p>
   232	      <div class="code">${safeOtp}</div>
   233	      <p>This code expires in 5 minutes. If you did not request it, you can safely ignore this email.</p>
   234	    `
   235	  );
   236	  const text = `${title}
   237	
   238	Code: ${otp}
   239	
   240	This code expires in 5 minutes. If you did not request it, you can safely ignore this email.`;
   241	
   242	  log.info('Sending OTP email', { email });
   243	
   244	  const result = await sendEmail({
   245	    to: email,
   246	    subject: title,
   247	    html,
   248	    text,
   249	  });
   250	
   251	  if (result.success) {
   252	    log.info('OTP email sent', { email, messageId: result.messageId });
   253	  }
   254	
   255	  return result;
   256	}
   257	
   258	function buildItemsRows(transaction: TransactionEmailData) {
   259	  const rows = transaction.items
   260	    .map((item, index) => {
   261	      const variant = item.variant?.name
   262	        ? `<br><small>${escapeHtml(item.variant.name)}</small>`
   263	        : '';
   264	      const unitPrice = formatPrice(Number(item.price));
   265	      const lineTotal = formatPrice(Number(item.price) * item.quantity);
   266	
   267	      return `
   268	        <tr>
   269	          <td>${index + 1}</td>
   270	          <td>${escapeHtml(item.product.name)}${variant}</td>
   271	          <td>${item.quantity}</td>
   272	          <td>${escapeHtml(unitPrice)}</td>
   273	          <td>${escapeHtml(lineTotal)}</td>
   274	        </tr>
   275	      `;
   276	    })
   277	    .join('');
   278	
   279	  return `
   280	    <table>
   281	      <thead>
   282	        <tr>
   283	          <th>#</th>
   284	          <th>Product</th>
   285	          <th>Quantity</th>
   286	          <th>Unit price</th>
   287	          <th>Line total</th>
   288	        </tr>
   289	      </thead>
   290	      <tbody>${rows}</tbody>
   291	    </table>
   292	  `;
   293	}
   294	
   295	function buildItemsText(transaction: TransactionEmailData): string {
   296	  return transaction.items
   297	    .map((item, index) => {
   298	      const variant = item.variant?.name ? ` (${item.variant.name})` : '';
   299	      const unitPrice = formatPrice(Number(item.price));
   300	      const lineTotal = formatPrice(Number(item.price) * item.quantity);
   301	
   302	      return `${index + 1}. ${item.product.name}${variant}
   303	   Quantity: ${item.quantity}
   304	   Unit price: ${unitPrice}
   305	   Line total: ${lineTotal}`;
   306	    })
   307	    .join('\n\n');
   308	}

   310	export async function sendBuyerOrderConfirmation(
   311	  transaction: TransactionEmailData
   312	): Promise<SendEmailResult> {
   313	  const buyerEmail = transaction.email;
   314	
   315	  log.info('Attempting to send buyer order confirmation', {
   316	    transactionCode: transaction.transactionCode,
   317	    buyerEmail,
   318	    hasEmail: !!buyerEmail,
   319	  });
   320	
   321	  if (!buyerEmail) {
   322	    log.info('No buyer email provided, skipping buyer confirmation email', {
   323	      transactionCode: transaction.transactionCode,
   324	    });
   325	    return {
   326	      success: false,
   327	      error: 'Buyer email not provided',
   328	    };
   329	  }
   330	
   331	  const buyerName =
   332	    transaction.user?.name || transaction.fullName || 'Customer';
   333	  const buyerPhone =
   334	    transaction.user?.phone || transaction.phone || 'Not provided';
   335	  const orderDate = formatDateTime(transaction.createdAt);
   336	  const totalItems = transaction.items.reduce(
   337	    (sum, item) => sum + item.quantity,
   338	    0
   339	  );
   340	  const total = formatPrice(Number(transaction.amount));
   341	  const subject = `Order ${transaction.transactionCode} confirmed - ${siteName}`;
   342	
   343	  const html = layoutEmail(
   344	    'Order confirmed',
   345	    `
   346	      <p>Hi ${escapeHtml(buyerName)},</p>
   347	      <p>Thanks for your order from ${escapeHtml(siteName)}. We received your payment and will process the order shortly.</p>
   348	      <div class="panel">
   349	        <strong>Order code:</strong> ${escapeHtml(transaction.transactionCode)}<br>
   350	        <strong>Order date:</strong> ${escapeHtml(orderDate)}<br>
   351	        <strong>Items:</strong> ${totalItems}<br>
   352	        <strong>Payment method:</strong> ${paymentMethodLabel(transaction.paymentMethod)}<br>
   353	        <strong>Total:</strong> ${escapeHtml(total)}
   354	      </div>
   355	      <h2>Shipping</h2>
   356	      <p>
   357	        <strong>Name:</strong> ${escapeHtml(buyerName)}<br>
   358	        <strong>Phone:</strong> ${escapeHtml(buyerPhone)}<br>
   359	        <strong>Address:</strong> ${escapeHtml(transaction.shippingAddress || 'Not provided')}<br>
   360	        ${
   361	          transaction.postalCode
   362	            ? `<strong>Postal code:</strong> ${escapeHtml(transaction.postalCode)}`
   363	            : ''
   364	        }
   365	      </p>
   366	      <h2>Order items</h2>
   367	      ${buildItemsRows(transaction)}
   368	      <div class="total">Total: ${escapeHtml(total)}</div>
   369	    `
   370	  );
   371	
   372	  const text = `Order confirmed
   373	
   374	Hi ${buyerName},
   375	
   376	Thanks for your order from ${siteName}. We received your payment and will process the order shortly.
   377	
   378	Order code: ${transaction.transactionCode}
   379	Order date: ${orderDate}
   380	Items: ${totalItems}
   381	Payment method: ${paymentMethodLabel(transaction.paymentMethod)}
   382	Total: ${total}
   383	
   384	Shipping
   385	Name: ${buyerName}
   386	Phone: ${buyerPhone}
   387	Address: ${transaction.shippingAddress || 'Not provided'}
   388	${transaction.postalCode ? `Postal code: ${transaction.postalCode}` : ''}
   389	
   390	Order items
   391	
   392	${buildItemsText(transaction)}
   393	
   394	Total: ${total}`;
   395	
   396	  const result = await sendEmail({
   397	    to: buyerEmail,
   398	    subject,
   399	    html,
   400	    text,
   401	  });
   402	
   403	  if (result.success) {
   404	    log.info('Buyer order confirmation sent', {
   405	      transactionCode: transaction.transactionCode,
   406	      buyerEmail,
   407	      messageId: result.messageId,
   408	    });
   409	  }
   410	
   411	  return result;
   412	}
   413	
   414	export async function sendAdminOrderConfirmation(
   415	  transaction: TransactionEmailData,
   416	  refId?: number
   417	): Promise<SendEmailResult> {
   418	  const adminEmail = process.env.ADMIN_EMAIL;
   419	
   420	  log.info('Attempting to send admin order confirmation', {
   421	    transactionCode: transaction.transactionCode,
   422	    adminEmailConfigured: !!adminEmail,
   423	  });
   424	
   425	  if (!adminEmail) {
   426	    log.warn('ADMIN_EMAIL not configured, skipping admin confirmation email');
   427	    return {
   428	      success: false,
   429	      error: 'ADMIN_EMAIL not configured',
   430	    };
   431	  }
   432	
   433	  const buyerName =
   434	    transaction.user?.name || transaction.fullName || 'Customer';
   435	  const buyerPhone =
   436	    transaction.user?.phone || transaction.phone || 'Not provided';
   437	  const buyerEmail =
   438	    transaction.user?.email || transaction.email || 'Not provided';
   439	  const accountType = transaction.isGuest
   440	    ? 'Guest checkout'
   441	    : 'Registered user';
   442	  const orderDate = formatDateTime(transaction.createdAt);
   443	  const totalItems = transaction.items.reduce(
   444	    (sum, item) => sum + item.quantity,
   445	    0
   446	  );
   447	  const total = formatPrice(Number(transaction.amount));
   448	  const subject = `New order ${transaction.transactionCode} - ${buyerName}`;
   449	
   450	  const html = layoutEmail(
   451	    'New order received',
   452	    `
   453	      <div class="panel">
   454	        <strong>Order code:</strong> ${escapeHtml(transaction.transactionCode)}<br>
   455	        <strong>Order date:</strong> ${escapeHtml(orderDate)}<br>
   456	        <strong>Items:</strong> ${totalItems}<br>
   457	        <strong>Payment method:</strong> ${paymentMethodLabel(transaction.paymentMethod)}<br>
   458	        ${refId ? `<strong>Payment reference:</strong> ${refId}<br>` : ''}
   459	        <strong>Total:</strong> ${escapeHtml(total)}
   460	      </div>
   461	      <h2>Customer</h2>
   462	      <p>
   463	        <strong>Name:</strong> ${escapeHtml(buyerName)}<br>
   464	        <strong>Phone:</strong> ${escapeHtml(buyerPhone)}<br>
   465	        <strong>Email:</strong> ${escapeHtml(buyerEmail)}<br>
   466	        <strong>Account type:</strong> ${accountType}
   467	      </p>
   468	      <h2>Shipping</h2>
   469	      <p>
   470	        <strong>Address:</strong> ${escapeHtml(transaction.shippingAddress || 'Not provided')}<br>
   471	        ${
   472	          transaction.postalCode
   473	            ? `<strong>Postal code:</strong> ${escapeHtml(transaction.postalCode)}`
   474	            : ''
   475	        }
   476	      </p>
   477	      <h2>Order items</h2>
   478	      ${buildItemsRows(transaction)}
   479	      <div class="total">Total: ${escapeHtml(total)}</div>
   480	    `
   481	  );
   482	
   483	  const text = `New order received
   484	
   485	Order code: ${transaction.transactionCode}
   486	Order date: ${orderDate}
   487	Items: ${totalItems}
   488	Payment method: ${paymentMethodLabel(transaction.paymentMethod)}
   489	${refId ? `Payment reference: ${refId}` : ''}
   490	Total: ${total}
   491	
   492	Customer
   493	Name: ${buyerName}
   494	Phone: ${buyerPhone}
   495	Email: ${buyerEmail}
   496	Account type: ${accountType}
   497	
   498	Shipping
   499	Address: ${transaction.shippingAddress || 'Not provided'}
   500	${transaction.postalCode ? `Postal code: ${transaction.postalCode}` : ''}
   501	
   502	Order items
   503	
   504	${buildItemsText(transaction)}
   505	
   506	Total: ${total}`;
   507	
   508	  const result = await sendEmail({
   509	    to: adminEmail,
   510	    subject,
   511	    html,
   512	    text,
   513	  });
   514	
   515	  if (result.success) {
   516	    log.info('Admin order confirmation sent', {
   517	      transactionCode: transaction.transactionCode,
   518	      adminEmail,
   519	      messageId: result.messageId,
   520	    });
   521	  }
   522	
   523	  return result;
   524	}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useToastStore, type Toast as ToastType } from '@/store/toast-store';
import AlertV4 from './Alert';

interface ToastItemProps {
  toast: ToastType;
  onRemove: (id: string) => void;
}

function ToastItem({ toast, onRemove }: ToastItemProps) {
  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
  const [isLeaving, setIsLeaving] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Trigger enter animation
    const showTimer = setTimeout(() => setIsVisible(true), 10);

    // Auto-dismiss after duration
    const duration = toast.duration ?? 4000;
    const dismissTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      setIsLeaving(true);
      setTimeout(() => onRemove(toast.id), 300);
    }, duration);

    return () => {
      clearTimeout(showTimer);
      clearTimeout(dismissTimer);
    };
  }, [toast.id, toast.duration, onRemove]);

  const handleClose = () => {
    setIsLeaving(true);
    setTimeout(() => onRemove(toast.id), 300);
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`
        transform transition-all duration-300 ease-out
        ${
          isVisible && !isLeaving
            ? 'translate-x-0 opacity-100'
            : '-translate-x-full opacity-0'
        }
      `}
    >
      <AlertV4
        type={toast.type}
        title={toast.title}
        onClose={handleClose}
        variant="soft"
        compact
        className="shadow-lg min-w-[280px] max-w-[380px]"
      >
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
          <span>{toast.message}</span>
          {toast.action && (
            <button
              onClick={() => {
                toast.action?.onClick();
                handleClose();
              }}
              className="self-start text-sm font-medium underline underline-offset-2 hover:no-underline transition-all"
            >
              {toast.action.label}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </AlertV4>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function ToastContainer() {
  const toasts = useToastStore((state) => state.toasts);
  const removeToast = useToastStore((state) => state.removeToast);

  if (toasts.length === 0) return null;

  return (
    <div
      className="fixed z-[9999] flex flex-col gap-3 pointer-events-none right-4 top-4"
      aria-live="polite"
      aria-label="اعلان‌ها"
    >
      {toasts.map((toast) => (
        <div key={toast.id} className="pointer-events-auto">
          <ToastItem toast={toast} onRemove={removeToast} />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

 export default async function Home() {
   // Fetch featured and discounted products directly from database
   // Using database-level filtering for optimal performance
   const [featuredProductsRaw, discountedProductsRaw] = await Promise.all([
     getFeaturedProducts({ limit: 4 }),
     getDiscountedProducts({ limit: 4 }),
   ]);
 
   let categories: Awaited<ReturnType<typeof getCategoryTree>> = [];
   try {
     categories = await getCategoryTree();
   } catch (error) {
     console.error('Failed to load category tree for homepage', error);
   }
 
   // Convert price and variant priceAdjust to number for display
   // Also ensure images is always an array (not null)
   const featuredProducts = featuredProductsRaw.map((p) => ({
     ...p,
     price: Number(p.price),
     images: p.images || [],
     variants: p.variants?.map((v) => ({
       ...v,
       priceAdjust: Number(v.priceAdjust),
     })),
   }));
   const discountedProducts = discountedProductsRaw.map((p) => ({
     ...p,
     price: Number(p.price),
     images: p.images || [],
     variants: p.variants?.map((v) => ({
       ...v,
       priceAdjust: Number(v.priceAdjust),
     })),
   }));
 
   // Get top 3 categories
   const topCategories = categories.slice(0, 3);
 
   return (
     <div className="min-h-screen bg-white">
       {/* Hero Section */}
       <section className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-12 md:py-20">
         <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-8 md:gap-12 items-center">
           <div className="order-2 md:order-1 text-right">

 import { Metadata } from 'next';
 import ProductList from '@/components/products/ProductList';
 import ProductsHero from '@/components/products/ProductsHero';

 export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic';
 
 interface ProductsPageProps {
   searchParams: Promise<{
     page?: string;
     category?: string;
     tag?: string;
     search?: string;
   }>;
 }
 
 export async function generateMetadata({
   searchParams,
 }: ProductsPageProps): Promise<Metadata> {
   const params = await searchParams;
   const { category, tag, search, page } = params;
 
   let title = 'محصولات - کیتیا';
   let description =
     'مشاهده و خرید بهترین لیوان‌های سفری و ماگ‌های باکیفیت. ارسال سریع، قیمت مناسب و کمک به گربه‌های خیابانی.';
 
   if (category) {
     title = `محصولات ${category} - کیتیا`;
     description = `مشاهده همه محصولات در دسته ${category}. لیوان‌های سفری و ماگ‌های باکیفیت با ارسال سریع.`;
   } else if (tag) {
     title = `محصولات با برچسب ${tag} - کیتیا`;
     description = `مشاهده محصولات با برچسب ${tag}. انتخاب از بین بهترین لیوان‌های سفری و ماگ‌ها.`;
   } else if (search) {
     title = `جستجو: ${search} - کیتیا`;
     description = `نتایج جستجو برای "${search}" در فروشگاه کیتیا.`;
   }
 
   if (page && parseInt(page) > 1) {
     title = `${title} - صفحه ${page}`;
   }
 
   // Build canonical URL with filters
   // For pagination, use page=1 as canonical (avoid duplicate content)
   // For filtered pages (category, tag, search), include those in canonical
   const canonicalPath = '/products';
   const queryParams: string[] = [];
 
   if (category) {
     queryParams.push(`category=${category}`);
   }
   if (tag) {
     queryParams.push(`tag=${tag}`);
   }
   if (search) {
     queryParams.push(`search=${encodeURIComponent(search)}`);
   }
 
   // Only add page to canonical if page > 1
   if (page && parseInt(page) > 1) {
     queryParams.push(`page=${page}`);
   }
 
   const canonicalUrl =
     queryParams.length > 0
       ? `${canonicalPath}?${queryParams.join('&')}`
       : canonicalPath;
 
   return {
     title,
     description,
     openGraph: {
       title,
       description,
       type: 'website',
-      locale: 'fa_IR',
+      locale: siteLocale.ogLocale,
       siteName: 'کیتیا',
       images: [
         {
           url: DEFAULT_OG_IMAGE,
           width: 1200,
           height: 630,
           alt: 'کیتیا - فروشگاه آنلاین',
         },
       ],
     },
     twitter: {
       card: 'summary_large_image',
       title,
       description,
       images: [DEFAULT_OG_IMAGE],
     },
     alternates: {
       canonical: getAbsoluteUrl(canonicalUrl),
     },
   };
 }
 
 export default async function ProductsPage() {
   const result = await getActiveProducts({
     page: 1,
     perPage: 20,
     sortBy: 'popular',
   });
 
   // Serialize Decimal prices to numbers for client components
   // Also ensure images is always an array (not null) and include createdAt, displayOrder for client-side sorting
   const products = result.data.map((product) => ({
     ...product,
     price: Number(product.price),
     images: product.images || [],
     discountPercent: product.discountPercent,
     isFeatured: product.isFeatured,
     createdAt: product.createdAt, // Include createdAt for client-side sorting
     displayOrder: product.displayOrder, // Include displayOrder for "popular" sorting
     variants: product.variants?.map((v) => ({
       ...v,
       priceAdjust: Number(v.priceAdjust),
       createdAt: v.createdAt,
     })),
   }));
 
   return (
     <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50">
       <main className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
         <ProductsHero />
 
         <ProductList
           initialProducts={products}
           initialPage={1}
           initialTotal={result.total}
         />
       </main>
     </div>
   );
 }

import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
import {
  validateEmail,
  validatePhone,
  detectIdentifierType,
  validateEmailUniqueness,
  validatePhoneUniqueness,
} from '@/services/user-service/validation';
import * as queries from '@/services/user-service/queries';

vi.mock('@/lib/logger', () => ({
  log: {
    info: vi.fn(),
    warn: vi.fn(),
    error: vi.fn(),
    debug: vi.fn(),
  },
}));

describe('user-service validation', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    vi.restoreAllMocks();
  });

  it('validates email and phone formats', () => {
    expect(validateEmail('user@example.com')).toBe(true);
    expect(validateEmail('not-an-email')).toBe(false);

    expect(validatePhone('09123456789')).toBe(true);
    expect(validatePhone('9123456789')).toBe(false);
  });

  it('detects identifier types', () => {
    expect(detectIdentifierType('user@example.com')).toBe('email');
    expect(detectIdentifierType('09123456789')).toBe('phone');
    expect(detectIdentifierType('invalid')).toBe('invalid');
  });

  it('rejects invalid or duplicate email', async () => {
    await expect(
      validateEmailUniqueness('bad-email')
    ).rejects.toThrow('فرمت ایمیل نامعتبر است');

    vi.spyOn(queries, 'checkUserExists').mockResolvedValue(true);
    await expect(
      validateEmailUniqueness('dup@example.com')
    ).rejects.toThrow('این ایمیل قبلاً استفاده شده است');
  });

  it('rejects invalid or duplicate phone', async () => {
    await expect(
      validatePhoneUniqueness('90123456789')
    ).rejects.toThrow('فرمت شماره تلفن نامعتبر است');

    vi.spyOn(queries, 'checkUserExists').mockResolvedValue(true);
    await expect(validatePhoneUniqueness('09123456789')).rejects.toThrow(
      'این شماره تلفن قبلاً استفاده شده است'
    );
  });

  it('passes when email/phone are undefined', async () => {
    await expect(validateEmailUniqueness(undefined)).resolves.toBeUndefined();
    await expect(validatePhoneUniqueness(undefined)).resolves.toBeUndefined();
  });
});

    24	/**
    25	 * Authenticate user with identifier (email or phone) and password
    26	 * @param identifier User email or phone number
    27	 * @param password User password
    28	 * @returns Authenticated user data
    29	 * @throws Error if authentication fails
    30	 */
    31	export async function authenticateUser(
    32	  identifier: string,
    33	  password: string
    34	): Promise<AuthUser> {
    35	  if (!identifier || !password) {
    36	    throw new Error('ایمیل/شماره تلفن و رمز عبور الزامی است');
    37	  }
    38	
    39	  try {
    40	    const identifierType = detectIdentifierType(identifier);
    41	
    42	    if (identifierType === 'invalid') {
    43	      throw new Error('فرمت ایمیل یا شماره تلفن نامعتبر است');
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    const supabase = createClient();
    47	
    48	    // Find user by email or phone
    49	    const userQuery = supabase.from('users').select('*').limit(1);
    50	    const { data: user, error } =
    51	      identifierType === 'email'
    52	        ? await userQuery.eq('email', identifier).maybeSingle()
    53	        : await userQuery
    54	            .in('phone', getPhoneLookupCandidates(identifier))
    55	            .maybeSingle();
    56	
    57	    if (error || !user) {
    58	      log.warn('Login attempt with non-existent identifier', {
    59	        identifier,
    60	        identifierType,
    61	      });
    62	      throw new Error('کاربری با این مشخصات یافت نشد');
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    // Check if user has a password (phone-only users might not have password)
    66	    if (!user.password) {
    67	      log.warn('Login attempt for user without password', {
    68	        identifier,
    69	        userId: user.id,
    70	      });
    71	      throw new Error('این حساب رمز عبور ندارد. لطفاً با پشتیبانی تماس بگیرید');
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    const isPasswordValid = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);
    75	
    76	    if (!isPasswordValid) {
    77	      log.warn('Login attempt with invalid password', {
    78	        identifier,
    79	        userId: user.id,
    80	      });
    81	      throw new Error('رمز عبور اشتباه است');
    82	    }
    83	
    84	    log.info('User authenticated successfully', {
    85	      identifier,
    86	      userId: user.id,
    87	    });
    88	
    89	    return {
    90	      id: user.id,
    80	
    81	  // Format as U-{6-digit number}
    82	  return `U-${nextNumber.toString().padStart(6, '0')}`;
    83	}

    85	/**
    86	 * Create a new user
    87	 * Supports both email and phone registration
    88	 */
    89	export async function createUser(data: {
    90	  email?: string;
    91	  phone?: string;
    92	  password?: string;
    93	  name: string;
    94	}): Promise<UserWithoutPassword> {
    95	  const { email, phone, password, name } = data;
    96	  const normalizedPhone = phone ? normalizePhoneNumber(phone) : undefined;
    97	
    98	  log.info('Creating user', { email, phone: normalizedPhone, name });
    99	
   100	  try {
   101	    // Validate at least one identifier
   102	    if (!email && !phone) {
   103	      throw new Error('ایمیل یا شماره تلفن الزامی است');
   104	    }
   105	
   106	    // Validate email if provided
   107	    if (email && !validateEmail(email)) {
   108	      log.warn('Invalid email format', { email });
   109	      throw new Error('فرمت ایمیل نامعتبر است');
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    // Validate phone if provided
   113	    if (phone && !validatePhone(phone)) {
   114	      log.warn('Invalid phone format', { phone });
   115	      throw new Error('فرمت شماره تلفن نامعتبر است');
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    // Validate password (required for email, optional for phone)
   119	    if (password && !validatePassword(password)) {
   120	      log.warn('Invalid password length', { email, phone });
   121	      throw new Error('رمز عبور باید حداقل ۸ کاراکتر باشد');
   122	    }
   123	
   124	    // Check if user already exists
   125	    const exists = await checkUserExists({ email, phone: normalizedPhone });
   126	    if (exists) {
   127	      log.warn('User already exists', { email, phone: normalizedPhone });
   128	      throw new Error(
   129	        'کاربری با این ایمیل یا شماره تلفن قبلاً ثبت‌نام کرده است'
   130	      );

   367	  userId: string,
   368	  data: {
   369	    name?: string;

   396	    if (data.name !== undefined) updateData.name = data.name;
   397	    if (data.email !== undefined) updateData.email = data.email || null;
   398	    if (data.phone !== undefined) updateData.phone = normalizedPhone || null;
   399	    if (data.shippingAddress !== undefined)
   400	      updateData.shippingAddress = data.shippingAddress;
   401	    if (data.postalCode !== undefined) updateData.postalCode = data.postalCode;
   402	
   403	    // Update user
   404	    const { data: updatedUser, error } = await supabase
   405	      .from('users')
   406	      .update(updateData)
   407	      .eq('id', userId)
   408	      .select(
   409	        'id, uid, email, phone, name, role, isVerified, shippingAddress, postalCode, createdAt, updatedAt'
   410	      )
   411	      .single();
   412	
   413	    if (error || !updatedUser) {
   414	      log.error('Failed to update user profile', { userId, error });
   415	      throw new Error('خطا در بروزرسانی پروفایل کاربر');
   416	    }
   417	
   418	    log.info('User profile updated successfully', { userId });
   419

     1	import { log } from '@/lib/logger';
     2	import { isValidPhoneNumber, normalizePhoneNumber } from '@/lib/utils/text';
     3	import { checkUserExists } from './queries';
     4	
     5	/**
     6	 * Validate email format
     7	 */
     8	export function validateEmail(email: string): boolean {
     9	  const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
    10	  return emailRegex.test(email);
    11	}
    12	
    13	export function validatePhone(phone: string): boolean {
    14	  return isValidPhoneNumber(phone);
    15	}
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * Detect if input is email or phone
    19	 */
    20	export function detectIdentifierType(
    21	  identifier: string
    22	): 'email' | 'phone' | 'invalid' {
    23	  if (validateEmail(identifier)) return 'email';
    24	  if (validatePhone(identifier)) return 'phone';
    25	  return 'invalid';
    26	}
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * Validate and check uniqueness for email
    30	 * Throws error if invalid or already exists
    31	 */
    32	export async function validateEmailUniqueness(
    33	  email: string | undefined,
    34	  excludeUserId?: string
    35	): Promise<void> {
    36	  if (email === undefined) return;
    37	
    38	  // Validate format
    39	  if (email && !validateEmail(email)) {
    40	    log.warn('Invalid email format', { email });
    41	    throw new Error('فرمت ایمیل نامعتبر است');
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  // Check uniqueness
    45	  if (email) {
    46	    const exists = await checkUserExists({ email }, excludeUserId);
    47	    if (exists) {
    48	      log.warn('Email already in use', { email });
    49	      throw new Error('این ایمیل قبلاً استفاده شده است');
    50	    }
    51	  }
    52	}
    53	
    54	/**
    55	 * Validate and check uniqueness for phone
    56	 * Throws error if invalid or already exists
    57	 */
    58	export async function validatePhoneUniqueness(
    59	  phone: string | undefined,
    60	  excludeUserId?: string
    61	): Promise<void> {
    62	  if (phone === undefined) return;
    63	
    64	  const normalizedPhone = phone ? normalizePhoneNumber(phone) : undefined;
    65	
    66	  if (phone && !validatePhone(phone)) {
    67	    log.warn('Invalid phone format', { phone });
    68	    throw new Error('فرمت شماره تلفن نامعتبر است');
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  if (normalizedPhone) {
    72	    const exists = await checkUserExists(
    73	      { phone: normalizedPhone },
    74	      excludeUserId
    75	    );
    76	    if (exists) {
    77	      log.warn('Phone already in use', { phone: normalizedPhone });
    78	      throw new Error('این شماره تلفن قبلاً استفاده شده است');
    79	    }
    80	  }
    81	}
    35	export function isValidName(name: string): boolean {
    36	  const trimmed = name.trim();
    37	  if (!trimmed) return false;
    38	  if (trimmed.length > 120) return false;
    39	
    40	  return /^[\p{L}\p{M}][\p{L}\p{M}\s.'-]*$/u.test(trimmed);
    41	}
    42	
    43	export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
    44	  if (!phone) return phone;
    45	
    46	  const defaultCountry = (
    47	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
    48	  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
    49	  let normalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
    50	
    51	  normalized = normalized.replace(/(?!^)\+/g, '');
    52	  if (normalized.startsWith('00')) {
    53	    normalized = `+${normalized.slice(2)}`;
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  try {
    57	    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
    58	    if (parsed?.isValid()) {
    59	      return parsed.number;
    60	    }
    61	  } catch {
    62	    return normalized;
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  return normalized;
    66	}
    67	
    68	export function getPhoneLookupCandidates(phone: string): string[] {
    69	  if (!phone) return [];
    70	
    71	  const defaultCountry = (
    72	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
    73	  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
    74	  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
    75	  const legacyNormalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
    76	  const legacyWithoutPlus = legacyNormalized.replace(/\+(?=.)/g, '');
    77	  const legacyIranianNumber = /^0\d{10}$/.test(legacyNormalized)
    78	    ? parsePhoneNumberFromString(legacyNormalized, 'IR')?.number
    79	    : undefined;
    80	  const nationalFormat = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry)
    81	    ?.formatNational()
    82	    .replace(/\D/g, '');
    83	
    84	  return Array.from(
    85	    new Set(
    86	      [
    87	        legacyIranianNumber,
    88	        normalized,
    89	        nationalFormat,
    90	        legacyNormalized,
    91	        legacyWithoutPlus,
    92	      ].filter((candidate): candidate is string => Boolean(candidate))
    93	    )
    94	  );
    95	}
    96	
    97	export function isValidPhoneNumber(phone: string): boolean {
    98	  if (!phone) return false;
    99	
   100	  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
   101	  const defaultCountry = (
   102	    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
   103	  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
   104	
   105	  try {
   106	    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
   107	    return parsed?.isValid() ?? false;
   108	  } catch {
   109	    return false;
   110	  }
   111	}

codex
The commit leaves existing unit tests inconsistent with the new email copy and default phone-country behavior, so the test suite will fail in a clean environment.

Full review comments:

- [P1] Update tests for neutral email subjects — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/email/client.ts:227-227
  With this new subject, `tests/unit/lib/email-client.test.ts` still expects `کد تایید کیتیا` (and the buyer confirmation test still expects the old Persian order subject), so the unit suite fails even though the implementation intentionally changed the copy. Update those assertions or preserve the old subject.

- [P1] Reconcile default phone country with validation tests — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/utils/text.ts:46-48
  This makes the no-env default `US`, but `tests/unit/services/user-service-validation.test.ts` still asserts `validatePhone('09123456789')` and `detectIdentifierType('09123456789')` are valid. In a clean CI environment with `NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY` unset, `isValidPhoneNumber` rejects that Iranian national number, so the unit suite fails; either set the test/env default to `IR` or update those expectations.
